country_event = {
	id = EAI_C.1
	hidden = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 2 }
	
	trigger = { 
		NOT = { has_country_flag = eai_construction }
		date > 1936.2.1
		is_ai = yes
	}
	
	immediate = {
		country_event = EAI_C.11
	}
	option = { name = "OK" }
}

country_event = {
	id = EAI_C.10
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		if = { limit = { num_of_civilian_factories < 40 } 									country_event = { id = EAI_C.11 months = 8 } }
		if = { limit = { num_of_civilian_factories < 50 num_of_civilian_factories > 39 } 	country_event = { id = EAI_C.11 months = 7 } }
		if = { limit = { num_of_civilian_factories < 60 num_of_civilian_factories > 49 } 	country_event = { id = EAI_C.11 months = 6 } }
		if = { limit = { num_of_civilian_factories < 80 num_of_civilian_factories > 59 } 	country_event = { id = EAI_C.11 months = 5 } }
		if = { limit = { num_of_civilian_factories < 100 num_of_civilian_factories > 79 } 	country_event = { id = EAI_C.11 months = 4 } }
		if = { limit = { num_of_civilian_factories > 99 } 									country_event = { id = EAI_C.11 months = 3 } }
	}
	option = { name = "OK" }
}

country_event = {
	id = EAI_C.50
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		if = { limit = { has_war = no date < 1938.4.1 }
			if = { limit = { num_of_civilian_factories < 60 } 									country_event = { id = EAI_C.51 months = 12 } }
			if = { limit = { num_of_civilian_factories < 80 num_of_civilian_factories > 59 } 	country_event = { id = EAI_C.51 months = 10 } }
			if = { limit = { num_of_civilian_factories < 100 num_of_civilian_factories > 79 } 	country_event = { id = EAI_C.51 months = 8 } }
			if = { limit = { num_of_civilian_factories > 99 } 									country_event = { id = EAI_C.51 months = 6 } }
		}
		if = { limit = { OR = { has_war = yes NOT = { date < 1938.4.1 } } }
			if = { limit = { num_of_civilian_factories < 60 } 									country_event = { id = EAI_C.51 months = 5 } }
			if = { limit = { num_of_civilian_factories < 80 num_of_civilian_factories > 59 } 	country_event = { id = EAI_C.51 months = 4 } }
			if = { limit = { num_of_civilian_factories < 100 num_of_civilian_factories > 79 } 	country_event = { id = EAI_C.51 months = 3 } }
			if = { limit = { num_of_civilian_factories > 99 } 									country_event = { id = EAI_C.51 months = 2 } }
		}
	}
	option = { name = "OK" }
}

country_event = {
	id = EAI_C.70
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		if = { limit = { OR = { has_idea = isolation has_idea = undisturbed_isolation } }
			if = { limit = { num_of_civilian_factories < 60 } 									country_event = { id = EAI_C.71 months = 10 } }
			if = { limit = { num_of_civilian_factories < 80 num_of_civilian_factories > 59 } 	country_event = { id = EAI_C.71 months = 9 } }
			if = { limit = { num_of_civilian_factories < 100 num_of_civilian_factories > 79 } 	country_event = { id = EAI_C.71 months = 8 } }
			if = { limit = { num_of_civilian_factories > 99 } 									country_event = { id = EAI_C.71 months = 7 } }
		}
		if = { limit = { NOT = { has_idea = isolation has_idea = undisturbed_isolation } }
			if = { limit = { num_of_civilian_factories < 60 } 									country_event = { id = EAI_C.71 months = 6 } }
			if = { limit = { num_of_civilian_factories < 80 num_of_civilian_factories > 59 } 	country_event = { id = EAI_C.71 months = 5 } }
			if = { limit = { num_of_civilian_factories < 100 num_of_civilian_factories > 79 } 	country_event = { id = EAI_C.71 months = 4 } }
			if = { limit = { num_of_civilian_factories < 120 num_of_civilian_factories > 99 } 	country_event = { id = EAI_C.71 months = 3 } }
			if = { limit = { num_of_civilian_factories < 140 num_of_civilian_factories > 119 } 	country_event = { id = EAI_C.71 months = 2 } }
			if = { limit = { num_of_civilian_factories > 139 } 									country_event = { id = EAI_C.71 months = 1 } }
		}
	}
	option = { name = "OK" }
}

country_event = {
	id = EAI_C.11
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		#1
		if = { limit = {
				NOT = { any_state = { is_controlled_by = ROOT free_building_slots = { building = industrial_complex size > 0 include_locked = no } free_building_slots = { building = arms_factory size > 0 include_locked = no } NOT = { is_in_home_area = yes } NOT = { any_neighbor_state = { controller = { has_war_with = ROOT } } } } }
				NOT = { any_state = { is_controlled_by = ROOT free_building_slots = { building = industrial_complex size > 0 include_locked = no } free_building_slots = { building = arms_factory size > 0 include_locked = no } NOT = { is_in_home_area = yes } NOT = { any_neighbor_state = { NOT = { is_controlled_by = ROOT } } } NOT = { any_neighbor_state = { controller = { has_war_with = ROOT } } } } } 
				NOT = { any_state = { is_controlled_by = ROOT free_building_slots = { building = industrial_complex size > 0 include_locked = no } free_building_slots = { building = arms_factory size > 0 include_locked = no } is_in_home_area = yes NOT = { any_neighbor_state = { controller = { has_war_with = ROOT } } } } }
				NOT = { any_state = { is_controlled_by = ROOT free_building_slots = { building = industrial_complex size > 0 include_locked = no } free_building_slots = { building = arms_factory size > 0 include_locked = no } is_in_home_area = yes NOT = { any_neighbor_state = { NOT = { is_controlled_by = ROOT } } } NOT = { any_neighbor_state = { controller = { has_war_with = ROOT } } } } } }
			random_state = { limit = { is_controlled_by = ROOT free_building_slots = { building = industrial_complex size > 0 include_locked = no } free_building_slots = { building = arms_factory size > 0 include_locked = no } } add_building_construction = { type = arms_factory level = 1 instant_build = no } }
		}
		if = { limit = { 
				any_state = { is_controlled_by = ROOT free_building_slots = { building = industrial_complex size > 0 include_locked = no } free_building_slots = { building = arms_factory size > 0 include_locked = no } NOT = { is_in_home_area = yes } NOT = { any_neighbor_state = { controller = { has_war_with = ROOT } } } } 
				NOT = { any_state = { is_controlled_by = ROOT free_building_slots = { building = industrial_complex size > 0 include_locked = no } free_building_slots = { building = arms_factory size > 0 include_locked = no } NOT = { is_in_home_area = yes } NOT = { any_neighbor_state = { NOT = { is_controlled_by = ROOT } } } NOT = { any_neighbor_state = { controller = { has_war_with = ROOT } } } } } 
				NOT = { any_state = { is_controlled_by = ROOT free_building_slots = { building = industrial_complex size > 0 include_locked = no } free_building_slots = { building = arms_factory size > 0 include_locked = no } is_in_home_area = yes NOT = { any_neighbor_state = { controller = { has_war_with = ROOT } } } } }
				NOT = { any_state = { is_controlled_by = ROOT free_building_slots = { building = industrial_complex size > 0 include_locked = no } free_building_slots = { building = arms_factory size > 0 include_locked = no } is_in_home_area = yes NOT = { any_neighbor_state = { NOT = { is_controlled_by = ROOT } } } NOT = { any_neighbor_state = { controller = { has_war_with = ROOT } } } } } }
			random_state = { limit = { is_controlled_by = ROOT NOT = { is_in_home_area = yes } NOT = { any_neighbor_state = { controller = { has_war_with = ROOT } } } free_building_slots = { building = industrial_complex size > 0 include_locked = no } free_building_slots = { building = arms_factory size > 0 include_locked = no } } add_building_construction = { type = arms_factory level = 1 instant_build = no } }
		}
		if = { limit = { 
				any_state = { is_controlled_by = ROOT free_building_slots = { building = industrial_complex size > 0 include_locked = no } free_building_slots = { building = arms_factory size > 0 include_locked = no } NOT = { is_in_home_area = yes } NOT = { any_neighbor_state = { NOT = { is_controlled_by = ROOT } } } NOT = { any_neighbor_state = { controller = { has_war_with = ROOT } } } } 
				NOT = { any_state = { is_controlled_by = ROOT free_building_slots = { building = industrial_complex size > 0 include_locked = no } free_building_slots = { building = arms_factory size > 0 include_locked = no } is_in_home_area = yes NOT = { any_neighbor_state = { controller = { has_war_with = ROOT } } } } }
				NOT = { any_state = { is_controlled_by = ROOT free_building_slots = { building = industrial_complex size > 0 include_locked = no } free_building_slots = { building = arms_factory size > 0 include_locked = no } is_in_home_area = yes NOT = { any_neighbor_state = { NOT = { is_controlled_by = ROOT } } } NOT = { any_neighbor_state = { controller = { has_war_with = ROOT } } } } } }
			random_state = { limit = { is_controlled_by = ROOT NOT = { is_in_home_area = yes } NOT = { any_neighbor_state = { NOT = { is_controlled_by = ROOT } } } free_building_slots = { building = industrial_complex size > 0 include_locked = no } free_building_slots = { building = arms_factory size > 0 include_locked = no } } add_building_construction = { type = arms_factory level = 1 instant_build = no } }

	id = EAI_C.12
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		#temp fix until trade is fixed
		if = { limit = { NOT = { has_war_with = SOV } } create_import = { resource = steel factories = 30 exporter = SOV } }
		if = { limit = { NOT = { has_war_with = ROM } } create_import = { resource = oil factories = 30 exporter = ROM } }
		
		country_event = { id = EAI_C.12 months = 1 }
	}
	option = { name = "OK" }
}

	id = EAI_C.32
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		#temp fix until trade is fixed
		if = { limit = { NOT = { has_war_with = GER } } create_import = { resource = steel factories = 30 exporter = GER } }

		if = { limit = { NOT = { has_war_with = USA } } create_import = { resource = aluminium factories = 30 exporter = USA } }

	}

}

country_event = {
	id = EAI_C.52
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		#temp fix until trade is fixed
		if = { limit = { NOT = { has_war_with = USA } } create_import = { resource = steel factories = 30 exporter = USA } }
		if = { limit = { NOT = { has_war_with = RAJ } } create_import = { resource = tungsten factories = 30 exporter = RAJ } }
		
		country_event = { id = EAI_C.52 months = 1 }
	}
	option = { name = "OK" }
}

#build AA if industry is maxed out

	id = EAI_C.100
	hidden = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 2 }

		num_of_available_civilian_factories > 10
		is_ai = yes

			is_controlled_by = ROOT 
			is_owned_by = ROOT

		}
